Since 1965, EF has been the world leader in international education. Today, we have 400 offices and schools in more than 50 countries with a network of 35,000 teachers and staff. We have helped millions of people of all ages and nationalities become global citizens, whether by learning a language, discovering the world, or earning an academic degree.	No matter where you are, from Paris to São Paulo, from Pusan to Perth, the need to learn a language and understand the world is stronger than ever before. The seed of EF was planted nearly 50 years ago, when Bertil Hult took a small group of Swedish students to England to study English. Now, EF has evolved with a compelling range of programs and services offered in more than 50 countries.	Our challenge is not to find the market. It’s to find the right people and grow the right managers to take advantage of the globalization of the world.	Join EF, the world leader in international education, and we promise you a rewarding career where you can make a difference. To keep up with our worldwide growth, we are looking to hire more global entrepreneurs who want to drive business, break new ground, and see the world. If you think this could be you, then contact us. The future could be closer than you think. 外包！需要在商汤科技公司驻场上班！	岗位职责：	1.负责Android ROM的软件研发。	2.参与Android ROM相关问题分析，定位，解决。	3.深入分析问题形成机制，持续优化android rom相关子系统。		任职要求：	1.两年以上Android开发经验，开发过成熟的Andriod产品；	2.熟悉Android OS体系结构，熟悉Android NDK、对Android框架有深刻的认识，有扎实的C/C++的语言基础；	3.熟悉Linux内核，熟悉Android Framework, HAL等软件框架，熟悉android surface, camera, media，network子系统优先考虑；	4.熟悉RK平台优先考虑。
